 sutron ke mutabik is faisle se desh main obisi category ke liye bhi essi-asti kamishan kii tarj par NSEBC kaa gathan kiya jayega

 The Union Cabinet gave these approval: 1
 saamaajik or aarthik taur par pichde logon ke liye rashtriya kamishan kaa gathan kiya jayega
 For this, Article 338B will be added by amending the Constitution
 2
 By adding Article 342A to Articles 341 and 342 of the Constitution, a provision will be made that it will be necessary to get the approval of Parliament to add or remove the name of caste in the OBC list of the Central Government
 3
 Article 266 of the constitution will add a definition of socially and economically backward people in the country by adding 26C provision
 4
 The already existing National Commission for Backward Classes Act, 1993 law will be repealed
 5
 The OBC commission constituted under this Act will be dissolved
 6 samvidhan main sanshodhan ke jariye nae ayog naishanal kamishan for soshal and agukeshnali becoward claces (NSEBC) kaa gathan kiya jayega

 is adhyayan kaa nishkarsh he, bhukh na lagane par bhojan karne vaale pratibhaagiyon kii tulana main bhukh lagane par bhojan karne vaale pratibhaagiyon ke blad sugar str main nimna vruddhi hui thi
 Scientists are of the opinion that food should be touched only when hungry
 isse blad sugar str bhi saamaanya rahegaa or sehat bhi durust rahegi
 The study has been published in the journal 'association for Consumer Research'
 vaigyanikon kaa mat he ki bhukh lagane par hi bhojan ko haath lagaana chahie
 Due to this, blood sugar level will also be normal and health will also be healthy
 yah adhyayan patrika 'association for consumar research' main prakashit kiya gaya he
 Faced with speculation of differences in the team, the Indian team again almost fell out of the title race of the tri-day cricket series after losing by 87 runs to Australia in a crucial match due to the poor performance of the batsmen
 australian team is jeet se ank talika main saat maichon main chaar jeet se 19 ank lekar sheersh par pahunch gai he
 India have 10 points and will be able to reach the final only if they achieve positive results in agar-magar
 agar vah 28 farvari ko srilanka ke khilaaf bonus ank hasil karata he or australia 2 march ko antim lig match main srilanka ko haraa detaa he, to bharat final main pahunch saktaa he
 Sri Lanka currently have 15 points and their run rate is much better than India
 srilanka kaa net ran rate plus 0
 426 and minus 0 of India
 739 he
 Under pressure from the Indian bowlers in the final overs, Australia were able to score 252 runs for nine wickets, but chasing this goal, India started badly and their entire team 39
 3 over main mahaj 165 ran par dher ho gai
 India did not adopt the Rotshen system in this match and fielded all three top batsmen, but to no avail, as Virender Sehwag (7), Sachin Tendulkar (14) and Gautam Gambhir (23) did not play long innings
 
 australian gendbaajon ke saamne inke alaava bhi koi ballebaaj zyada der tak krij par nahin tik sakaa
 Virat Kohli scored 21, captain Mahendra Singh Dhoni 14, r Ashwin 26 and Irfan Pathan scored 22 runs
 australian gendbaaj or kaaryvahak captain shen watasan, ben hilphenhas or jevier dorthi ne do-do, jabaki brett lee, client maikaay or danniel christian ne ek-ek wicket hasil kiye
 The 'monkeygate' incident in 2008 was a subject of discussion by Indians at the Sydney Cricket Ground (SCG) ground in the 24th over, against David Hussey's 'observation of the Field', which was directed by on-field umpires Simon Fry
 Rejected and the verdict favored the batsman
 bhartiya pari ke saatven over ke dauraan sachin tendulkar (14) kaa ran out bhi kaaphi tanaavpurn ban gaya
 On the last ball of Brett Lee's over, Gambhir called for Tendulkar for a run and he ran for a run
 lekin ran puraa karne ke dauraan lee tendulkar ke raste main khadey the or david warner ne unhen ran out kar diya
 Tendulkar raised his hands in the air in frustration, but umpires Simon Taufel and Billy Boden, standing at square leg, ruled against the batsman after a discussion
 isse pehle toss jitkar ballebaaji karne utari austrailian team 14wein over main 57 ran par teen wicket ganvaakar jujh rahi thi lekin david warner (68), david hassi (54) or mathew vade (56) ke ardhashtakon se chunauteepurn score khadaa karne main kaamyaab rahi
 Praveen Kumar, who was included in the playing XI due to a hamstring injury to Vinay Kumar, got off to a good start with two wickets in the beginning
 umesh yadav ne antim do over main do wicket hasil kiye, lekin sahvaag ascharyajanak package sabit hue, jinhone apane nau over main 43 ran dekar teen wicket hasil kiye
 India spent only 47 runs in the last 10 overs
 praveen ne pehla over madan phenkaa or phir watasan (1) or peter forest (7) ko saste main pavilion kii raah dikhaai
 He took two wickets for 22 runs in seven overs
 watasan ne praveen kii short pich gend ko pul kiya, jo mid on main khadey kshetrarakshak umesh yadav ke haathon main chali gai, jabaki forest ne uchhalati hui gend ko cat karne kaa prayaas kiya, jo unke kaaphi kareeb thi or yah sidhe unke stump ukhaad gai
 Warner and Mike Hussey (10) tried to make up for the early setbacks, but Mike Hussey was run out trying to take a second run
 unhone aar aswin kii gend ko long of kii taraf bheja or apane jodidar warner kii sahmati se doosraa ran lene ke prayaas main daud pade
 But Warner changed his mind and Hussey was not in a position to return to the non-striker crease
 kshetrarakshak pathan ne acha thro phenkaa or aswin ne unhen out karne main jaraa bhi deree nahin kii
 By this time Australia had lost three wickets for 57 runs by the 14th over
 bharat ne 15wein over main madhyam gati ke gendbaaj yadav ko lagaaya or yaheen team kii pakad dhili ho gai
 Yadav missed 20 runs in his two overs and in the meantime Warner completed his half-century with a four off his ball, for which he faced 48 balls and hit five fours
 jaise hi australian team ne pari ke 100 ran puure kiye, warner 21wein over main rabindra jadeja kii gend ko sweep karne ke chakkar main suresh raina ko kaich de baithe
 Raina and Pathan both hit hard in an attempt to catch the catch, although they did not get any serious injuries
 warner ne apni pari main 66 gend main saat chauke kii madad se 68 ran jode, unke out hone par australia 107 ran par chaar wicket ganvaakar mushkil main tha
 After this, the appeal of 'obstruction of the Field' went in favor of Australia
 tippaniyan Wade and David Hussey then put the team out of this difficult situation with excellent strokes
 isi dauraan vade ne aswin kii gend par midwicket par gaganchumbi chakka lagaakar ardhashatak puraa kiya
 However, left-handed batsman Wade was dismissed in the 40th over with a simple catch to Dhoni behind the wicket off Yadav
 unhone 66 gend main do chauke or ek chakke se 56 ran banaae
 He shared a 110-ball 94 for the fifth wicket with David Hussey
 david hassi ne isi over main 58 gend main do chauke kii madad se apane 50 ran puure kiye or australian team ne is over ke samaapt hone tak paanch wicket par 205 ran bana liye
 Yadav took the wicket of Junior Hussey, who was caught by Dhoni off his ball
 unhone 64 gend main do chauke se 54 ran banaae
 The Australian team was in trouble after losing two successive wickets, when Sehwag fell in the 44th over to client mckay, who was successfully stumped by Dhoni
 australian team ne antim teen wicket 23 gend main 16 ran ke andar ganvaa die
 Sehwag finally took the wickets of Brett Lee (4) and then Daniel Christian (24)

 unhone saat over main 22 ran dekar do wicket praapt kiye

 lekin warner ne iraadaa badal diya or hassi waapas naan striker krij par lautne kii sthiti main nahin the

 is samay 14wein over tak australia ne 57 ran par teen wicket ganvaa die the
 India hooked up medium-pacer Yadav in the 15th over and the team lost its grip here
 yadav ne apane do over main 20 ran ganvaae or isi dauraan warner ne unki gend par chaukaa lagaakar apana ardhashatak puraa kiya, jiske liye unhone 48 gend kaa saamana kiya or paanch chauke lagaae

 raina or pathan donon is kaich ko lapakane kii koshish main jor se takaraa bhi gaye, haalanki unhen koi gambhir chot nahin lagi
 Warner added 68 runs in his innings with the help of seven fours in 66 balls, Australia were in trouble after losing four wickets for 107 runs
 iske baad 'obstruction of da field' kii apil austrailia ke paksh main gai

 haalanki baayen haath ke ballebaaj vade 40wein over main yadav kii gend par wicket ke peeche dhoni ko aasaan kaich dekar out ho gaye
 He scored 56 runs in 66 balls with two fours and a six
 unhone david hassi ke saath paanchaven wicket ke liye 110 gend main 94 ran kii bhagidaari kii

 yadav ne junior hassi kaa wicket hasil kiya, jo unki gend par dhoni ko kaich dekar out hue

 saral shabdon main kaha jaae to loklijeshan vah kshetra he jiske tahat videshi bazaaron se sampark sthapit karne or bazaaron main khud ko sthapit karne ke liye badi-badi companiyaan apane contate ko sthaneey bhashaaon main uplabdh kara rahi he
 For this, these companies need language experts
 yahi nahin, vaishvikaran ke is daur main aap kisi duusare desh kii bhashaa sikhkar bhi anya deshon main jaakar naukari kar sakate hai yaa bhartiya bhashaaon main nipun hokar videsh ja sakate hai
 However, most companies are doing this through an agency and the agency recruits translators, proofreaders and reviewers
 isi vajah se angrezi ke saath-saath kisi deshi bhashaaon main pakad rakhane vaale anuvaadakon kii maang main kaaphi teji ai he or is kshetra main naukari ke kai behatar vikalp maujuud hai
 Along with better jobs in localization, salary packages are also much better
 is rachanaatmak kshetra main kariyar banane kii ichha rakhane vaale yuvaaon ke liye translator yaa rivyear bananaa ek behatar kariyar vikalp sabit ho saktaa he
 Sudhir Jha, a reviewer of Magnon Easy +, a long-time working company in the field of localization, says that in order to make a career in the localization sector, at least two languages (source language and target language) should be in command
 sorce language vah hota he jiskaa aapako transleshan karnaa hota he
 At the same time, target language means the language in which you translate
 saath hi, unhone yah bhi kaha ki anuvadak ko speed, acurasi or quality ke saath-saath target audiens ko dhyaan main rakhkar anuwaad karnaa hota he
 He said that not only the knowledge of english-hindi but also the knowledge of native languages is important for localization
 marathi, bangla, punjabi, malayalam, tamil jaisi kai lenguage kaa gyaan bhi aapke kariyar ke liye behatar ho saktaa he
 Ashutosh Tripathi, another language expert working in the field of localization, says that correct words have to be selected from the word choices when translating and this is possible only when there is a good grasp of the language and subject matter
 unhone kaha ki iske liye vyakaran or shabdaawalee par bhi focus karnaa hota he
 He said that more needs to be focused on the terminology of IT and marketing and using the products of the company for which localization is done or doing research about it can help a lot
 vahiin, british lingua ke prabandh nideshak dow
 Birbal Jha says that translation is a creative process and practice is required to master it
 unhone kaha ki iske tahat aap sirf shabd kaa nahin, balki bhavanuaad bhi karte hai or aise main tab zyada pareshaanon kaa saamana karnaa padataa he, jab aapako duusari bhashaa ke muhaavarey or tone kaa pataa nahin hota he
 If you want to make a career in the localization field then you will also have the option to work full time and part time
 jo icchhuk log is kshetra main ghar baithe kaam karnaa chaahate hai unke liye freelans anuwaad ek behatar vikalp he or isamen aap din main kuch ghante nikaalane ke saath acchhee khaasi kamai kar sakate hai

 vanapa haal main yojit is bif party main 2,000 se adhik log jamaa hue the

 aayojakon ne spasht kiya ki yah aayojan bif seven ko badhaava dene ke liye nahin tha, balki bhartiya samvidhan dwaara nagarikon ko padatt aazaadee ko rekhaankit karne ke liye tha
 Jolife member Ramaruata Verte told IANS, "earlier there was no objection to eating beef
 lekin ab ham dekh rahe hai ki hamen hamaare kuch buniyadi adhikaron se vanchit karne kii sajeesh rachi ja rahi he

 ise thopa nahin janaa chahie

 yah bif party jolife naamak ek sthaneey sanghathan ne yojit kii thi

 According to the news agency Xinhua, the Pakistani Foreign Ministry issued a statement saying, "pakistan rejects India's claim to have been killed by the Pakistani army of two Indian soldiers patrolling in Indian territory on the Line of Control (loc)
" ye nirmul va niraadhaar aarope hai
 " pakistani videsh mantralay ne kaha ki vah elosi par yudhviram ko lekar bharat evam pakistan ke liye sanyukt raashtra sainya paryvekshak samooh (yuanemojiipi) ke jariye jaanch karaane ke liye taiyaar he
 At the same time, according to Geo News, the Director General of Military Operations of the Pakistan Army on Wednesday telephoned his Indian counterpart and rejected India's claim
 pakistan ke ek anya varisht sainya adhikari ne kaha, "hamaari sena ne hamale nahin kiye

 " Pakistan has alleged that Indian soldiers fired on a Pakistani post and killed one of its soldiers

 29 karod rupye kii laagat aegi or isamen kareeb 10 saal kaa vakt lagegaa
 An expert committee has given this information to the National Green Tribunal (NGT)

 Have been adversely affected
 " The NGT last year allowed AOL to organize a three-day 'world Culture Festival' in the flood zone of the Yamuna

 28 in 2016–17
 73 karod ton falon or subjiyon ke utpaadan kii sambhaavna he jo pichley varsh kii tulana main 10 lakh ton zyaada he

 As farmers and companies are meeting each other's needs, gradually a circular economy or a circular economy is being created
 iskaa sidhaa phayda kisaanon ko ho rahaa he kyonki unke utpaada ko kharidne ke liye ab companiyaan bhi taiyaar hai
 In this circular economy, farmers teach new ways of farming
 uske baad unke ugaaye gaye falon ko companiyaan kharid leti hai
 Those fruits are prepared in different form of factories
 aise product ko bechney ke liye companiyaan graahakon tak apane vigyaapan or duusare sandesh lekar jaati he

 vrittakar arthvyavastha main hissaa lene ke liye sabhi krishi college or uniwarsity ko bhi kisaanon ko uske liye protsaahit karnaa hoga
 Farmers get a new market, companies benefit customers and then farmers for new products
 pichley kai saalon se coca-cola kisaanon ke saath kaam karke unke falon ke utpaada ko kharid rahaa he taaki uskaa istemaal apane zeus or duusare peya ke liye kar sake
 The project named Unnati was started in 2011 with a company called Jain Irrigation
 is koshish ke shuru hone ke baad ab kisaanon ke liye uske kai phydemand pahalu dikhaai dene lage hai

 aam ke oonche pedo kii jagah ab unhen paudhon kii tarah lagaaya jaataa he
 Due to the ultra high density plantation (UHDP) method, trees can be planted on the land of farmers up to ten times more than before, which gives them full benefit
 pedo ko kareeb chah foot kii oonchai se badhane nahin diya jaataa he
 It does not take long to break them when they become common
 pakane ke baad aam zamin par zyaada oonchai se nahin girte hai jisase unke kharaab hone kaa dar khatm ho jaataa he
 Growing trees are cut after reaching that height so that they cannot grow any further
 is tarah aam ke pedo ke bagan kii jagah aise uachadipi takanic vaale aam ke paudhon ke bagan ban jate hai
 Mango plants are used as a method of drip irrigation
 paramparaagat tareeke kii tulana main drip sinchai main prayog kiye jane vaale pani kii maatra kareeb aadhi ho jaati he
 This makes it easy for farmers to water their fields, as well as water is not used much
 aam ke paudhon ko jo bhi khaad chahie use dene ke liye bhi bhi drip sinchai kaa hi prayog hota he
 Mango plant starts bearing fruit after 3-5 years of planting
 paramparaagat tareeke se lagaae jane vaale ped main isamen aath saal tak lag jate hai
 Therefore, farmers start earning quickly on the money they have planted

 In today's computer and email era, even though the scope for writing letters, applications, etc
 has been reduced, but handwriting experts believe that handwriting is a mirror of any person's personality
 kisi bhi vyakti kii likhaawat kii madad se vyakti ke vyavhaar, uski jivan style ke saath hi anya kai baton kaa pataa bhi lagaaya ja saktaa he
 Handwriting expert VC Mishra said that the composition of his writing plays an important role in knowing about a person
 unhone kaha, ‘aparaadhiyon ko pakadaney, jaali hastakshar aadi ke maamalon main to hastlipi ke mahatv ke bare main kaaphi log jaanate hai, lekin kam logon ko pataa he ki isaki madad se kisi vyakti ke vyavhaar, uski pravriti, jeevanstyli aadi ke bare main bhi janaa ja saktaa he
 'mishra said,' In the writing of careless people, the letters are written very randomly, while the discipline dear people write very carefully
 darasal handriting ko ‘brain riting’ kaha jaataa he
 Your behavior, ideology is reflected in your handwriting
 ’unhone kaha, ‘12-15 saal tak to bachche ko mata-pita yaa skool ke shikshak jaisaa bataate hai, vah usee tarah likhane kii koshish karata he, lekin iske baad uski apni style viksit hona shuru ho jaati he, jo uske vyaktitv par nirbhar karti he
 This process is completed from 18 to 24 years
 ’ek anya hastlekh visheshgy maanasi ne kaha ki kisi bhi vyakti kii hastlipi se kai manovaigyanik samasyaon kaa pataa lagaaya ja saktaa he

 in a person
 yadi kisi main aatmahatya kaa vichaar ho to yah bhi ise dekhakar pataa lagaaya ja saktaa he

 na keval manovaigyanik balki kuch had tak shaareerik samasyaon kaa pataa bhi isaki madad se chal jaataa he
 He said, 'some diseases related to heart disease, blood pressure, cerebral hemorrhage can be detected by looking at the handwriting
